<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy_and_influence">Legacy and influence</span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:25%;&#32;; background-color: #CCDDFF;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r856303512">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:360px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{min-width:100%;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"<i>Harry Potter</i> was in the vanguard of a new approach to big-budget film-making. Most modern blockbuster franchises have two things in common: they are based on known properties such as books and comics, and they are steered by respected but little-known directors."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<i><a href="/wiki/The_Economist" title="The Economist">The Economist</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-&#91;&#91;The_Economist&#93;&#93;_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-[[The_Economist]]-150">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>The <i>Harry Potter</i> films and their success have been retrospectively considered to have had a significant impact on the <a href="/wiki/Film_industry" title="Film industry">film industry</a>. They are cited as having helped redefine the <a href="/wiki/Blockbuster_(entertainment)" title="Blockbuster (entertainment)">Hollywood blockbuster</a> in the 21st century by initiating a shift toward established <a href="/wiki/Media_franchise" title="Media franchise">media franchises</a> forming the basis of successful films. In the wake of the final film's release, Claudia Puig of <i><a href="/wiki/USA_Today" title="USA Today">USA Today</a></i> wrote that the films "inspired every major studio to try to capture [its] alchemic formula, spawning a range of copycats and wannabes" and "also have shown Hollywood how to make a glossy blockbuster with an eye toward keeping costs down."<sup id="cite_ref-&#91;&#91;USA_Today&#93;&#93;_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-[[USA_Today]]-151">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> A 2009 article from <i><a href="/wiki/The_Economist" title="The Economist">The Economist</a></i> argued that the films were "in the vanguard" of adaptations of established properties being the modern film franchise model, citing <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings_(film_series)" title="The Lord of the Rings (film series)">The Lord of the Rings</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Spider-Man_in_film#Sam_Raimi_films" title="Spider-Man in film">Spider-Man</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Batman_in_film#Christopher_Nolan" title="Batman in film">The Dark Knight Trilogy</a></i> as examples of successful film series that followed <i>Harry Potter</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s suit.<sup id="cite_ref-&#91;&#91;The_Economist&#93;&#93;_150-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-[[The_Economist]]-150">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, the practice of splitting the finale of a film series into two <a href="/wiki/Back_to_back_film_production" class="mw-redirect" title="Back to back film production">back-to-back films</a> began with the success of <i><a href="/wiki/Production_of_Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Production of Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a></i>, and it would soon be replicated by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hobbit:_The_Desolation_of_Smaug" title="The Hobbit: The Desolation of Smaug">The Hobbit: The Desolation of Smaug</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hobbit:_The_Battle_of_the_Five_Armies" title="The Hobbit: The Battle of the Five Armies">The Battle of the Five Armies</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Twilight_Saga:_Breaking_Dawn_%E2%80%93_Part_1" title="The Twilight Saga: Breaking Dawn – Part 1">The Twilight Saga: Breaking Dawn – Parts 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Twilight_Saga:_Breaking_Dawn_%E2%80%93_Part_2" title="The Twilight Saga: Breaking Dawn – Part 2">2</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hunger_Games:_Mockingjay_%E2%80%93_Part_1" title="The Hunger Games: Mockingjay – Part 1">The Hunger Games: Mockingjay – Parts 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hunger_Games:_Mockingjay_%E2%80%93_Part_2" title="The Hunger Games: Mockingjay – Part 2">2</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Avengers:_Infinity_War" title="Avengers: Infinity War">Avengers: Infinity War</a></i> and its <a href="/wiki/Untitled_Avengers_film" title="Untitled Avengers film">untitled sequel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-&#91;&#91;The_Hollywood_Reporter&#93;&#93;_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-[[The_Hollywood_Reporter]]-152">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The films are also widely credited with singlehandedly signalling the popularity of films based on <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_literature" title="Children&#39;s literature">children's</a> and <a href="/wiki/Young_adult_fiction" title="Young adult fiction">young adult literature</a> in the 2000s and 2010s, correlating with the book series' own literary influence. Costance Grady and Aja Romano, commenting on the whole <i>Harry Potter</i> franchise's legacy for <i><a href="/wiki/Vox_(website)" title="Vox (website)">Vox</a></i> in light of its 20th anniversary, wrote that youth-targeted literature has since become "a go-to well of ideas for Hollywood," pointing to the successes of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Twilight_Saga_(film_series)" title="The Twilight Saga (film series)">The Twilight Saga</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hunger_Games_(film_series)" title="The Hunger Games (film series)">The Hunger Games</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-&#91;&#91;Vox_(website)&#124;Vox&#93;&#93;_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-[[Vox_(website)|Vox]]-153">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The series has spawned a vast volume of fan fiction, with nearly 600 thousand inspired stories catalogued.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup>  Youtube hosts many fan films, ranging from amateur productions to full length films.
</p>
